</font><font color="#C0C0C0">Benedicto moves in towards you in a grabbing posture.
Benedicto lifts you triumphantly into the air, then yanks you down into his
 raised knee with back breaking force.
With a sickening crunch, a bolt of pure agony erupts from your back.  Your head
 lolls to one side and you lose all the feeling in your legs.  As you crumple
 to the ground you realise that the throw did, indeed, snap your spine like a
 dry twig.
You have been slain by Benedicto.
